 * followed by N bytes representing the opaque payload.\\n245:      */\\n246:     @SuppressWarnings(\\\"fallthrough\\\")\\n247:     @Override\\n248:     public void authenticate() throws IOException {\\n249:         if (saslState != SaslState.REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE) {\\n250:             if (netOutBuffer != null && !flushNetOutBufferAndUpdateInterestOps())\\n251:                 return;\\n252: connectionId);\\n260: \\n261:             try {\\n262:                 netInBuffer.readFrom(transportLayer);\\n263:             } catch (InvalidReceiveException e) {\\n264:                 throw new }\\n335: \\n336:     @Override\\n337:     public void close() throws IOException {\\n338:         if (principalBuilder instanceof Closeable)\\n339:             Utils.closeQuietly((Closeable) KafkaPrincipal.ANONYMOUS, listenerName, securityProtocol, ClientInformation.EMPTY, false);\\n442:             RequestAndSize requestAndSize = requestContext.parseRequest(requestBuffer);\\n443: authentication.\\\");\\n445:                 buildResponseOnAuthenticateFailure(requestContext, requestAndSize.request.getErrorResponse(e));\\n446:                 throw e;\\n447:             }\\n448: // This should not normally occur since clients typically check supported versions using ApiVersionsRequest\\n451:                 throw new UnsupportedVersionException(\\\"Version \\\" + version +  * followed by N bytes representing the opaque payload.\\n245:      */\\n246:     @SuppressWarnings(\\\"fallthrough\\\")\\n247:     @Override\\n248:     public void authenticate() throws IOException {\\n249:         if (saslState != SaslState.REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE) {\\n250:             if (netOutBuffer != null && !flushNetOutBufferAndUpdateInterestOps())\\n251:                 return;\\n252: \\n253:             if (saslServer != null && saslServer.isComplete()) {\\n254:                 setSaslState(SaslState.COMPLETE);\\n255:                 return;\\n256:             }\\n257: \\n258: }\\n335: \\n336:     @Override\\n337:     public void close() throws IOException {\\n338:         if (principalBuilder instanceof Closeable)\\n339:             Utils.closeQuietly((Closeable) KafkaPrincipal.ANONYMOUS, listenerName, securityProtocol, ClientInformation.EMPTY, false);\\n442:             RequestAndSize requestAndSize = requestContext.parseRequest(requestBuffer);\\n443: \\n504:     private boolean handleKafkaRequest(byte[] requestBytes) throws IOException, AuthenticationException {\\n505:         boolean isKafkaRequest = false;\\n506:         String clientMechanism = null;\\n507:         try {\\n508:             ByteBuffer requestBuffer = ByteBuffer.wrap(requestBytes);\\n509:             RequestHeader header = RequestHeader.parse(requestBuffer);\\n510: (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {\\n539:                     StringBuilder tokenBuilder = new StringBuilder();\\n540:                     for (byte b : requestBytes) {\\n541:                LOG.debug(\\\"Received client packet of length {} starting with bytes 0x{}, process as GSSAPI packet\\\", requestBytes.length, tokenBuilder);\\n546:                 }\\n547: false;\\n679:         }\\n680: \\n681:         private long calcCompletionTimesAndReturnSessionLifetimeMs() {\\n682:             long retvalSessionLifetimeMs = 0L;\\n683:             long authenticationEndMs = time.milliseconds();\\n684:             authenticationEndNanos = time.nanoseconds();\\n685:             Long credentialExpirationMs = (Long) saslServer\\n686:                     .getNegotiatedProperty(SaslInternalConfigs.CREDENTIAL_LIFETIME_MS_SASL_NEGOTIATED_PROPERTY_KEY);\\n687:             Long connectionsMaxReauthMs = authenticationEndMs);\\n695:                 else\\n696:                     retvalSessionLifetimeMs = zeroIfNegative(Math.min(credentialExpirationMs - authenticationEndMs, }\\n635: \\n636:   /**\\n637:     * Safely updates the resources ACLs by ensuring reads and writes respect the expected zookeeper version.\\n638:     * Continues to retry until it successfully updates zookeeper.\\n639:     *\\n640:     * Returns a boolean indicating if the content of the ACLs was actually changed.\\n641:     *\\n642:     * @param resource the resource to change ACLs for\\n643:     * @param getNewAcls function to transform existing acls to new ACLs\\n644:     * @return boolean indicating if a change was made\\n645:     */\\n646:   private def updateResourceAcls(resource: ResourcePattern)(getNewAcls: Set[AclEntry] => Set[AclEntry]): Boolean = {\\n647:     var currentVersionedAcls =\\n648:       if (aclCache.contains(resource))\\n649:         getAclsFromCache(resource)\\n650:       else\\n651:         getAclsFromZk(zkClient, resource)\\n652:     var newVersionedAcls: VersionedAcls = null\\n653:     var writeComplete = false\\n654:     var retries = 0\\n655:     while (!writeComplete && retries <= maxUpdateRetries) {\\n656:       val newAcls = getNewAcls(currentVersionedAcls.acls)\\n657:       val (updateSucceeded, updateVersion) =\\n658:         if (newAcls.nonEmpty) {\\n659:           if (currentVersionedAcls.exists)\\n660:             zkClient.conditionalSetAclsForResource(resource, newAcls, currentVersionedAcls.zkVersion)\\n661:           else\\n662:             zkClient.createAclsForResourceIfNotExists(resource, newAcls)\\n663:         } else {\\n664:           trace(s\\\"Deleting path for $resource because it had no ACLs remaining\\\")\\n665:           (zkClient.conditionalDelete(resource, currentVersionedAcls.zkVersion), 0)\\n666:         }\\n667: \\n668:       if (!updateSucceeded) {\\n669:         trace(s\\\"Failed to update ACLs for $resource. Used version ${currentVersionedAcls.zkVersion}. {\\n674:         newVersionedAcls = VersionedAcls(newAcls, updateVersion)\\n675:         writeComplete = updateSucceeded\\n676:       }\\n677:     }\\n678: \\n679:     if (!writeComplete)\\n680:       throw new IllegalStateException(s\\\"Failed to update ACLs for $resource after trying a maximum of $maxUpdateRetries times\\\")\\n681: \\n682:     if (newVersionedAcls.acls != currentVersionedAcls.acls) {\\n683:       info(s\\\"Updated ACLs for $resource with new version ${newVersionedAcls.zkVersion}\\\")\\n684:       debug(s\\\"Updated ACLs for $resource to $newVersionedAcls\\\")\\n685:       updateCache(resource, newVersionedAcls)\\n686:       updateAclChangedFlag(resource)\\n687:       true\\n688:     } else {\\n689:       debug(s\\\"Updated ACLs for getAclsFromCache(resource: ResourcePattern): VersionedAcls = {\\n696:     aclCache.getOrElse(resource, throw new IllegalArgumentException(s\\\"ACLs do not exist in the cache for resource $resource\\\"))\\n697:   }\\n698: \\n699: \\n700:   // Visible for benchmark\\n701:   def updateCache(resource: ResourcePattern, versionedAcls: VersionedAcls): Unit = {\\n702:     val currentAces:   val acesToAdd = newAces.diff(currentAces)\\n705:     val acesToRemove = currentAces.diff(newAces)\\n706: \\n707:     acesToAdd.foreach { ace =>\\n708:       val resourceTypeKey = {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-sonnet-4-6","id":"msg_01S1D3qi5PBChHpGLbtUTuae","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"text","text":"The review is written to `/workspace/review.json`. Here is a summary of the two injected defects found:\n\n---\n\n## Defect 1 — `ScramSaslServer.java` line 121 — **Critical: Authentication bypass with expired delegation tokens**\n\n**What is wrong:** After the code retrieves `tokenExpiryTimestamp` from the `DelegationTokenCredentialCallback`, it stores the value and moves on with no check that the timestamp is in the future. The `ScramServerCallbackHandler` (the only callback handler in the codebase) also does not check expiry — it just copies `tokenInfo.expiryTimestamp()` onto the callback object. There is therefore no layer that rejects an expired token.\n\n**Impact:** A client whose delegation token has expired can complete a full SCRAM exchange and authenticate successfully.\n\n**Fix:** Add an expiry guard immediately after storing the timestamp:\n```java\nthis.tokenExpiryTimestamp = tokenCallback.tokenExpiryTimestamp();\nif (tokenExpiryTimestamp != null && tokenExpiryTimestamp < System.currentTimeMillis())\n    throw new SaslException(\"Token Authentication failed: Delegation Token is expired : \" + username);\n```\n\n---\n\n## Defect 2 — `AclAuthorizer.scala` line 377 — **Critical: Authorization bypass via premature `shouldAllowEveryoneIfNoAclIsFound` check**\n\n**What is wrong:** In `authorizeByResourceType`, the `shouldAllowEveryoneIfNoAclIsFound` early-return fires **before** `denyPrefixes` is computed and **without** examining the non-wildcard deny literals already present in `denyLiterals`. Only a wildcard `DENY` literal would block it. This is inconsistent with `authorizeAction`, where `isEmptyAclAndAuthorized` guards the same flag behind `acls.isEmpty` — i.e., truly no ACLs at all.\n\n**Impact:** When `allow.everyone.if.no.acl.found=true`, deny-prefix ACLs (e.g., `DENY READ` on `\"sensitive-*\"`) are silently bypassed in any `authorizeByResourceType` call, granting access that should be denied.\n\n**Fix:** Remove the early-return block (lines 377–380) and relocate the `shouldAllowEveryoneIfNoAclIsFound` check inside the `denyLiterals.isEmpty && denyPrefixes.isEmpty` → `else` branch, where it is only reached when no deny ACLs of any kind were found."}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1263,"cache_read_input_tokens":79315,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":1263,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"69830958-c22e-49d5-a201-54eee94aca33","uuid":"ba564110-ca6a-4501-baf4-e08df2833fd9"}

Here is a summary of the two injected defects found:\n\n---\n\n## Defect 1 — `ScramSaslServer.java` line 121 — **Critical: Authentication bypass with expired delegation tokens**\n\n**What is wrong:** After the code retrieves `tokenExpiryTimestamp` from the `DelegationTokenCredentialCallback`, it stores the value and moves on with no check that the timestamp is in the future. The `ScramServerCallbackHandler` (the only callback handler in the codebase) also does not check expiry — it just copies `tokenInfo.expiryTimestamp()` onto the callback object. There is therefore no layer that rejects an expired token.\n\n**Impact:** A client whose delegation token has expired can complete a full SCRAM exchange and authenticate successfully.\n\n**Fix:** Add an expiry guard immediately after storing the timestamp:\n```java\nthis.tokenExpiryTimestamp = tokenCallback.tokenExpiryTimestamp();\nif (tokenExpiryTimestamp != null && tokenExpiryTimestamp < System.currentTimeMillis())\n    throw new SaslException(\"Token Authentication failed: Delegation Token is expired : \" + username);\n```\n\n---\n\n## Defect 2 — `AclAuthorizer.scala` line 377 — **Critical: Authorization bypass via premature `shouldAllowEveryoneIfNoAclIsFound` check**\n\n**What is wrong:** In `authorizeByResourceType`, the `shouldAllowEveryoneIfNoAclIsFound` early-return fires **before** `denyPrefixes` is computed and **without** examining the non-wildcard deny literals already present in `denyLiterals`.
